 monsoon kii barish abtak saamaanya ke mukaable 103 fisadi rahi he
 That means more rain than usual
 behtareen barish kaa sidhaa asar hamaare desh ke kisaanon kii fasal par padataa he
 This time the effect of good rains is visible on the sowing of kharif crops
 ab tak kharif fasalon kaa buvaai rakabaa pichley saal ke mukaable takreeban 58
 27 lakh hectares has been more
 joardaar barish se buvaai kshetra badhakrishi mantralay ke taaja aankadon ke mutabik ab tak kharif kaa kul buvaai kshetra 954
 Has exceeded 18 lakh hectares, while this figure last year 895
 91 lakh hectare tha
 Sowing of Kharif crop is believed to be the biggest reason behind the excessive rainfall from July to August
 ganga-yamuna ke maidani ilaakon se lekar madhya bharat ke pathari ilaakon tak monsoon joardaar rahaa he
 Due to this, farmers sowed kharif crops extensively
 daalen ho sakati he sastiis baar mahangi daalon se kuch had tak nijaat mil sakati he
 The thing is that this year, pulses sowing area has seen a tremendous increase
 pichley saal 13 agast tak daalon kii buvaai 97
 There were 74 lakh hectares of area
 lekin kharif sijan main is baar dalhan fasalon kaa buvaai rakabaa 130
 There has been 17 lakh hectares
 iskaa sidhaa sa matlab ye hua ki is samay daalon kii badi hui keemton or achche monsoon kaa asar daal kii buvaai par bhi dikh rahaa he
 This is likely to reduce the prices of pulses this time in the coming months
 krishi mantralay ke aankadon par agar bharosa karen to achche monsoon kaa acha asar fasalon par najar aayega
 For farmers, paddy is the main crop of relief season and its dependence on monsoon is to a large extent

 Kharif sowing of cereal grains also increased by about 10 lakh hectares this year from the previous year to 173
 56 lakh hectare darj kii gai he

 25 lakh hectare ho gaya he

 asipi raghuveer ne kaha ki wo log aise maamalon kii jaanch kar rahe hai or abhi tak kii jaanch se pataa chalaa he ki aise phone dilli se aae the
 Everyone has heard about fraudulently swapping SIM cards, that is, making duplicate sims, but is it possible that just by sending a message to the phone or pressing a few buttons, the information on your SIM card reaches another place and your duplicate SIM How to make a card? When we talked to the experts of Cyber security about this, it came to know that it is not easy to do but not impossible
 sibar security export saket modi se jab hamane is bare main poocha to unhone kaha ki aise kisi cese se kabhi unka vaasta to nahin padaa he lekin yah nahin kaha ja saktaa ki aisa sambhav nahin he
 But when we inquired more about this, it came to know that many years ago Carsten Knoll of Germany, a world-renowned cyber security expert, while presenting his research about this, said that without coming in contact with phone, even from far SIM card can be hacked
 unhone is bare main apni research 2013 main pesh kii thi or aagaah kiya tha ki kai mobile companiyaan abhi bhi puraani technology par aadhaarit sim card istemaal kar rahi hai jinhen sirf massej bhejkar hack kiya ja saktaa he
 Knoll's research was much discussed at the time and was also presented at the famous Black Hat conference for cyber security
 sim kii jaankaree churaane ko lekar tamaam bank apane graahakon ko lagaataar aagaah karte rahete hai
 Now the question arises as to how money can be withdrawn from a bank account as a SIM card becomes a duplicate
 darasal sim card hack karne vaale apradhi unheen logon ko nishaanaa banaate hai jinke bank ditels or tamaam duusari jaankariyaan pehle se unke paas hoti hai
 Such criminals do their work in many stages and choose their victims accordingly
 # sabase pehle ye log farji mail or massej ke jariye yaa phiranphishingke jariye kisi ke naam, pataa, phone number or bank acount sambandhit sari jaankaree juta lete hai
 # Then these people collect all the information about that person from social media like Facebook, Twitter, such as - Birthday, family name, Aadhaar card number, PAN number and all other information
 inhen jaankariyon ke aadhaar par wo bank ke password kaa andaja lagane kii koshish karte hai yaa phir tamaam jaankariyon ke aadhaar par password riset kar dete hai
 Here now OTP is required for which SIM card comes handy
 # phir farji pahchaan patr ke aadhaar par yah log usee vyakti ke naam par doosraa dupliket sim card hasil kar lete hai jiske liye vah mobile operator ko yah bataate hai ki unka phone yaa sim card kho gaya he
 # After the duplicate sim card is in hand, these people log into the bank account and also get OTP on the basis of duplicate sim
 is bich phone band hone kii vajah se jis vyakti kaa bank acount he use yah pataa tak nahin chal paata ki uske bank acount kaa otipi dupliket sim card par aa rahaa he or uske bank se paise nikal rahe hai
 # By the time the person reaches the mobile company or bank, the criminals are caught doing their job
 sibar export or bank kii suraksha se jude log aise dhokhe se bachane ke liye kuch baton kaa dhyaan rakhane par jor dete hai
 1
 kisi bhi anjaan vyakti ke email ko soch samajhakar kholen, khaas taur par agar usamen koi atachament ho to use haragij naa kholen

 2

 If in doubt, call the bank and find out or inform the police about that number
 kisi ke kehane par naa to koi massej bhejein or naa hi koi phone kaa koi batan dabaaen
 3
 apane bank ke acount main log in karne ke liye sidhe khud bank acount kaa adress tip karen
 Never visit the bank's site based on the address provided in an email
 yah nakli site ho sakati he
 4
 soshal media par soch samajhakar kar koi bhi jaankaree daalen kyonki koi bhi is jaankaree kaa galat phayda uthaa saktaa he
 5
 kabhi agar achaanak phone par anaap-shanaap phone aane lage or koi lagaataar ghanti bajaane lage to kabhi bhi tang hokar phone band nahin karen balki saavdhaan ho jaaen

" " Obama said, "my administration will provide all necessary help to the officers involved in the investigation of the incident
" " Obama said, "michelle and i were deeply saddened to hear of the tragic incident of the shooting in Wisconsin

 "krishna said that he has spoken to Indian Ambassador Nirupama Rao after the incident

 Describing the Sikhs as a part of the broader American family, Obama promised in a statement issued by the White House that his administration would fully assist in investigating Sunday's incident

 " obama ne kaha, "meraa prashasan ghatana kii jaanch se jude adhikariyon ko sabhi aavashyak madad muhaiyaa karaayega

 Romney said that he and his wife Anne are with heartbroken victims, their families and the entire Sikh community in Oak Creek

 obama ne kaha he, "ek dharmik sthal par ghati is ghatana par shok manaate hue hamen yaad he ki sikhon ne hamaare desh ko kitna samrudh banaaya he, jo hamaare vyapak america parivaar ke hissaa hai
 " obama ne kaha, "meraa prashasan ghatana kii jaanch se jude adhikariyon ko sabhi aavashyak madad muhaiyaa karaayega
 " obama ne kaha, "visconsin main golibari kii trasadpurn ghatana ke bare main sunakar mishael or mujhe gaharaa dukh hua
 " obama ke republican pratidwandvi mit romany ne boston main ise 'hinsa kii nirmam karrwai' or ek traasadee qaraar diya, jise kisi bhi dharmik sthal par kabhi nahin ghatana chahie
 Romney said that he and his wife Anne are with heartbroken victims, their families and the entire Sikh community in Oak Creek
 pradhanmantri manmohan singh ne ghatana par gaharaa shok prakat karte hue aashaa vyakt kii he ki america prashasan hamale kii jaanch karegaa or yah sunishchit karaayega ki is tarah kii ghatana bhavishya main na ghate
 Speaking to reporters in the Parliament House, Manmohan said, "the brutal killing of people gathered in a religious gathering is a very sad incident
 " Manmohan said, "I hope the US administration will investigate the reasons behind this brutal attack on the devotees and ensure that such a horrific incident does not happen in future
" main aashaa karata hum ki sakasham adhikari ghatana kii jaanch karenge or prabhavit pariwaron ko raahat muhaiyaa karaayenge
 i express my heartfelt condolences to the families of those killed and injured in the incident
 " Foreign Minister SM Krishna has condemned the attack on Sunday at a gurdwara in the US
 unhone kaha ki america main sikh samudaay ne apane kaam ke prati khud ke drushtikon or patibaddhta ke jariye vahaan ke prashasan va logon kaa sammaan hasil kiya he
 Krishna said, "I condemn this incident
 " krishna ne kaha ki ghatana ke baad unhone bhartiya rajdoot nirupama raav se baat kii he
 Minister of State for External Affairs Praneet Kaur said that gurdwaras and other religious places in the community in America should be taken care of
 cor ne kaha, "yah ek bahut hi stabdhkaari or tragedeepurn ghatana ghati he, jo nindaneey he
 We are in equal contact with the US government and our Ambassador Nirupama Rao has sent a special officer from Washington to Wisconsin and Consul General in Chicago is also monitoring the case
 " The US embassy on Monday expressed deep grief over the incident that killed six Sikh devotees in an attack at a gurdwara in Wisconsin
 duutavas se jari bayaan main kaha gaya he, "america duutavas ke sadsy america or bharat ke sikh samudaay ke prati sahanubhuti evam shok samvednaa jaahir karne main raashtrapati (baraak) obama ke saath hai
 "comments bayaan main kaha gaya he, "hamaara hriday, hamaari aatma or prarthana peediton va unke parijanon ke saath he
 An investigation into the incident has begun
 is tarah kii koi bhi ghatana trasadpurn he, khaastaur se jab vah kisi dharmasthal par ghate
 America takes the responsibility of respect and protection of people of all religions very seriously
 " The statement said, "religious freedom and religious tolerance are fundamental pillars of American society
 america main sikh samudaay is siddhant main yogadan karata he or america ke saamaajik taane-bane ko arthpurna majbootee pradaan karata he
 " america atorni james santel ke hawaale se kaha gaya he ki yah spasht nahin he ki yah gharelu aatankwaad he yaa nahin
 He said, "my focus is not on what kind of crime it is, but the focus is on this incident and the deaths of people
" " City Police Chief John Edwards said that around 10 on Sunday morning
 30 baje ok creek sthit gurudware main hui golibari kii ghatana ko gharelu aatankwaad jaisi ek ghatana maani ja rahi he
 The officer who was the first to respond was also injured in the incident
 edwards ne kaha ki ok creek ke jo police adhikari 911 kii kol ke jawaab main gaye the, ve ek peedit kii madad kar rahe the tabhi hamalavar ne unamem se ek adhikari par hamalaa bol diya or us par kai goliyaan barasaai
 In response, another police officer fired and killed the attacker
 jarnal centinel ne jaanch se sambandhit ek sutara ke hawaale se kaha he ki hamalavar shwet purush tha, jisaki umr 40 varsh ke aasapaas rahi hogi
 He was retired from the army
 sutara ne kaha ki ghatnasthal se ek aagneyastra or kai magazine baraamad hue hai

 " shahar ke police pramukh jon edwards ne kaha ki ravivaar subah lagbhag 10
 The shooting incident at the gurdwara at Oak Creek at 30 am is considered as an incident like domestic terrorism
 is ghatana main sarvapratham pratikriya dene vaala adhikari bhi ghayal ho gaya
 Edwards said police officers from Oak Creek who went in response to a 911 call were helping a victim when the attacker attacked one of the officers and fired several shots at him
 jawaab main ek duusare police adhikari ne golibari kar hamalavar ko maar daalaa
 The Journal Sentinel quoted a source as saying that the attacker was a white male, who must have been around 40 years of age
 vah sena se sevamukt ho gaya tha
 The source said that a firearms and several magazines have been recovered from the scene
 aparaahn 4
 At 30 pm, Obama received a call from Governor Scott Walker, Oak Creek Mayor Steve Scheffidi and Charanjit Singh, a trustee of the gurdwara, and expressed condolences to the dead and concern for the injured
 sikhon ko vyapak america parivaar kaa ek hissaa bataate hue obama ne white house kii ore se jari ek bayaan main vaada kiya ki ravivaar kii ghatana kii jaanch main unka prashasan puri madad karegaa
 Obama has said, "we mourn the incident at a religious site, remembering how prosperous the Sikhs have been to our country, who are part of our wider American family
" " Obama said, "my administration will provide all necessary help to the officers involved in the investigation of the incident
" " Obama said, "michelle and i were deeply saddened to hear of the tragic incident of the shooting in Wisconsin
 " Obama's Republican rival Mitt Romney called it a 'ruthless action of violence' and a tragedy in Boston, which should never happen at any religious site
 romany ne kaha ki vah or unki patni ain hriday se peediton, unke pariwaron or puure ok creek ke sikh samudaay ke saath hai
 Prime Minister Manmohan Singh expressed deep condolences over the incident and hoped that the US administration would investigate the attack and ensure that such incidents do not happen in future
 sansad bhawan main samvaadadaataaon se baatcheet main manmohan ne kaha, "dharmik sabha main jamaa hue logon kii nirmam hatya bahut hi dukhad ghatana he
 " manmohan ne kaha, "mujhe aashaa he ki america prashasan shraddhaluon par hue is krur hamale ke peeche ke kaarnon kii jaanch karegaa or yah sunishchit karaayega ki is tarah kii khaufnak ghatana bhavishya main na ho
 i hope that the competent authorities will investigate the incident and provide relief to the affected families
 ghatana main maare gaye or ghayal hue logon ke parijanon ke prati main apni hardik samvednaa vyakt karata hum
 " videsh mantri esaem krishna ne america main ek gurudware main ravivaar ko hue hamale kii ninda kii he
 He said that the Sikh community in America has gained the respect of the administration and the people through its attitude and commitment to its work
 krishna ne kaha, "main is ghatana kii ninda karata hum
 "krishna said that he has spoken to Indian Ambassador Nirupama Rao after the incident
 videsh rajya mantri pranit cor ne kaha ki america main sthit gurudwaron or samudaay ke anya dharmik sthalon kaa khyaal rakhaa janaa chahie
 Kaur said, "it has been a very shocking and tragic incident, which is condemnable
" ham america sarkaar se baraabar sampark main hai or hamaari rajdoot nirupama raav ne washington se ek vishesh adhikari ko visconsin bheja he tathaa chicago main mahavanijyadoot bhi maamle par najar rakhe hue hai
 " america duutavas ne visconsin ke gurudware main hue hamale main chah sikh shraddhaluon ke maare jane kii ghatana par somvaar ko gaharaa dukh vyakt kiya
 The statement issued from the embassy said, "the members of the US embassy are with President (barack) Obama in expressing sympathy and condolences to the Sikh community of America and India
" "tippaniyan The statement said, "our heart, our soul and prayers are with the victims and their families
 ghatana kii jaanch shuru ho gai he
 Any such incident is tragic, especially when it happens at a shrine
 america sabhi dharm ke logon ke sammaan or hifaazat kii jimmedaari bahut gambheertha se letaa he
 " bayaan main kaha gaya he, "dharmik aazaadee or dharmik sahishnutaa america samaaj ke buniyadi stambh hai

 " america duutavas ne visconsin ke gurudware main hue hamale main chah sikh shraddhaluon ke maare jane kii ghatana par somvaar ko gaharaa dukh vyakt kiya
 The statement issued from the embassy said, "the members of the US embassy are with President (barack) Obama in expressing sympathy and condolences to the Sikh community of America and India
" "tippaniyan The statement said, "our heart, our soul and prayers are with the victims and their families
 ghatana kii jaanch shuru ho gai he
 Any such incident is tragic, especially when it happens at a shrine
 america sabhi dharm ke logon ke sammaan or hifaazat kii jimmedaari bahut gambheertha se letaa he
 " bayaan main kaha gaya he, "dharmik aazaadee or dharmik sahishnutaa america samaaj ke buniyadi stambh hai
 The Sikh community in America contributes to this theory and provides meaningful reinforcement to the social fabric of America
 " Obama has said, "we mourn the incident at a religious site, remembering how prosperous the Sikhs have been to our country, who are part of our wider American family
" " Obama said, "my administration will provide all necessary help to the officers involved in the investigation of the incident
" " Obama said, "michelle and i were deeply saddened to hear of the tragic incident of the shooting in Wisconsin
 " Obama's Republican rival Mitt Romney called it a 'ruthless action of violence' and a tragedy in Boston, which should never happen at any religious site
 romany ne kaha ki vah or unki patni ain hriday se peediton, unke pariwaron or puure ok creek ke sikh samudaay ke saath hai
 Prime Minister Manmohan Singh expressed deep condolences over the incident and hoped that the US administration would investigate the attack and ensure that such incidents do not happen in future
 sansad bhawan main samvaadadaataaon se baatcheet main manmohan ne kaha, "dharmik sabha main jamaa hue logon kii nirmam hatya bahut hi dukhad ghatana he
 " manmohan ne kaha, "mujhe aashaa he ki america prashasan shraddhaluon par hue is krur hamale ke peeche ke kaarnon kii jaanch karegaa or yah sunishchit karaayega ki is tarah kii khaufnak ghatana bhavishya main na ho
 i hope that the competent authorities will investigate the incident and provide relief to the affected families
 ghatana main maare gaye or ghayal hue logon ke parijanon ke prati main apni hardik samvednaa vyakt karata hum
 " videsh mantri esaem krishna ne america main ek gurudware main ravivaar ko hue hamale kii ninda kii he
 He said that the Sikh community in America has gained the respect of the administration and the people through its attitude and commitment to its work
 krishna ne kaha, "main is ghatana kii ninda karata hum
 "krishna said that he has spoken to Indian Ambassador Nirupama Rao after the incident
 videsh rajya mantri pranit cor ne kaha ki america main sthit gurudwaron or samudaay ke anya dharmik sthalon kaa khyaal rakhaa janaa chahie

 " Manmohan said, "I hope the US administration will investigate the reasons behind this brutal attack on the devotees and ensure that such a horrific incident does not happen in future
" main aashaa karata hum ki sakasham adhikari ghatana kii jaanch karenge or prabhavit pariwaron ko raahat muhaiyaa karaayenge

 " Foreign Minister SM Krishna has condemned the attack on Sunday at a gurdwara in the US
 unhone kaha ki america main sikh samudaay ne apane kaam ke prati khud ke drushtikon or patibaddhta ke jariye vahaan ke prashasan va logon kaa sammaan hasil kiya he
 Krishna said, "I condemn this incident
 " krishna ne kaha ki ghatana ke baad unhone bhartiya rajdoot nirupama raav se baat kii he
 Minister of State for External Affairs Praneet Kaur said that gurdwaras and other religious places in the community in America should be taken care of
 cor ne kaha, "yah ek bahut hi stabdhkaari or tragedeepurn ghatana ghati he, jo nindaneey he
 We are in equal contact with the US government and our Ambassador Nirupama Rao has sent a special officer from Washington to Wisconsin and Consul General in Chicago is also monitoring the case
 " The US embassy on Monday expressed deep grief over the incident that killed six Sikh devotees in an attack at a gurdwara in Wisconsin
 duutavas se jari bayaan main kaha gaya he, "america duutavas ke sadsy america or bharat ke sikh samudaay ke prati sahanubhuti evam shok samvednaa jaahir karne main raashtrapati (baraak) obama ke saath hai
 "comments bayaan main kaha gaya he, "hamaara hriday, hamaari aatma or prarthana peediton va unke parijanon ke saath he
